## ğŸ¯ Executive Summary

**Vision:**
> The ultimate mod management experience for Valheim - fast, beautiful, and intelligent.

**Core Principles:**
1. **Performance First** - Handle 1000+ mods without lag
2. **Zero Configuration** - Auto-detect everything possible
3. **Beautiful by Default** - Modern, polished UI
4. **Safe & Reliable** - Never lose user data
5. **Community-Driven** - Share and discover modpacks

**Target Users:**
- **Casual Modders** (60%) - Want 5-10 mods, easy setup
- **Enthusiasts** (30%) - Manage 50-100 mods, multiple profiles
- **Content Creators** (10%) - Create modpacks, share with community

---

## ğŸ› ï¸ Tech Stack

### Frontend
```json
{
  "framework": "SolidJS 1.8+",
  "language": "TypeScript 5.3+",
  "styling": "Tailwind CSS 3.4+",
  "ui_library": "Kobalte (headless)",
  "animations": "Motion One",
  "icons": "Lucide Solid",
  "state": "Solid Store (built-in)",
  "router": "Solid Router",
  "build": "Vite 5+"
}
```

### Backend
```json
{
  "desktop_framework": "Tauri 2.0",
  "backend_language": "Rust 1.75+",
  "python_bridge": "PyO3 0.20+",
  "database": "SQLite (rusqlite)",
  "async_runtime": "Tokio",
  "http_client": "reqwest",
  "serialization": "serde"
}
```

### Python Integration (Optional)
```json
{
  "purpose": "Reuse existing mod_manager.py logic",
  "method": "PyO3 bindings OR sidecar process",
  "fallback": "Pure Rust rewrite (preferred)"
}
```

## ğŸ¨ UI/UX Design System

### Color Palette

```scss
// Dark Theme (Default)
$colors-dark: (
  // Base
  background-primary: #0f0f0f,      // Main background
  background-secondary: #1a1a1a,    // Cards, panels
  background-tertiary: #252525,     // Hover states
  
  // Surface
  surface-elevated: #2d2d2d,        // Elevated cards
  surface-overlay: rgba(0,0,0,0.8), // Modals, dropdowns
  
  // Text
  text-primary: #ffffff,
  text-secondary: #b4b4b4,
  text-tertiary: #888888,
  text-disabled: #555555,
  
  // Accent
  accent-primary: #3b82f6,          // Blue - primary actions
  accent-secondary: #8b5cf6,        // Purple - secondary
  accent-success: #10b981,          // Green - success
  accent-warning: #f59e0b,          // Orange - warning
  accent-error: #ef4444,            // Red - errors
  accent-info: #06b6d4,             // Cyan - info
  
  // Borders
  border-subtle: #2d2d2d,
  border-default: #404040,
  border-strong: #555555,
  
  // Special
  profile-vanilla: #4a90e2,
  profile-combat: #e24a4a,
  profile-building: #4ae290,
  profile-magic: #904ae2,
  profile-exploration: #e2904a,
);

// Light Theme (Optional)
$colors-light: (
  background-primary: #ffffff,
  background-secondary: #f5f5f5,
  text-primary: #1a1a1a,
  // ... (inverse of dark)
);
```

### Typography

```scss
// Font Stack
$font-family-sans: 'Inter', 'Segoe UI', system-ui, sans-serif;
$font-family-mono: 'JetBrains Mono', 'Fira Code', monospace;

// Type Scale
$typography: (
  // Display
  display-large: (
    size: 3.5rem,      // 56px
    weight: 700,
    line-height: 1.1,
    letter-spacing: -0.02em,
  ),
  
  // Headings
  heading-1: (
    size: 2.5rem,      // 40px
    weight: 700,
    line-height: 1.2,
  ),
  heading-2: (
    size: 2rem,        // 32px
    weight: 600,
    line-height: 1.3,
  ),
  heading-3: (
    size: 1.5rem,      // 24px
    weight: 600,
    line-height: 1.4,
  ),
  
  // Body
  body-large: (
    size: 1.125rem,    // 18px
    weight: 400,
    line-height: 1.6,
  ),
  body-default: (
    size: 1rem,        // 16px
    weight: 400,
    line-height: 1.5,
  ),
  body-small: (
    size: 0.875rem,    // 14px
    weight: 400,
    line-height: 1.5,
  ),
  
  // UI
  label: (
    size: 0.875rem,
    weight: 500,
    line-height: 1.4,
  ),
  caption: (
    size: 0.75rem,     // 12px
    weight: 400,
    line-height: 1.4,
  ),
);
```

### Spacing System

```scss
// 8px base unit
$spacing: (
  0: 0,
  1: 0.25rem,    // 4px
  2: 0.5rem,     // 8px
  3: 0.75rem,    // 12px
  4: 1rem,       // 16px
  5: 1.25rem,    // 20px
  6: 1.5rem,     // 24px
  8: 2rem,       // 32px
  10: 2.5rem,    // 40px
  12: 3rem,      // 48px
  16: 4rem,      // 64px
  20: 5rem,      // 80px
  24: 6rem,      // 96px
);
```

### Component Design Tokens

```scss
// Buttons
$button: (
  height-small: 32px,
  height-default: 40px,
  height-large: 48px,
  
  padding-x-small: 12px,
  padding-x-default: 16px,
  padding-x-large: 24px,
  
  radius: 8px,
  radius-full: 9999px,
  
  transition: all 0.2s ease,
);

// Cards
$card: (
  padding: 24px,
  radius: 12px,
  shadow: 0 2px 8px rgba(0,0,0,0.1),
  shadow-hover: 0 4px 16px rgba(0,0,0,0.15),
);

// Inputs
$input: (
  height: 40px,
  padding-x: 12px,
  radius: 8px,
  border-width: 1px,
  focus-ring: 0 0 0 3px rgba(59, 130, 246, 0.1),
);
```

### Animation Guidelines

```scss
// Timing Functions
$ease-out-expo: cubic-bezier(0.16, 1, 0.3, 1);
$ease-in-out-circ: cubic-bezier(0.85, 0, 0.15, 1);
$ease-spring: cubic-bezier(0.68, -0.55, 0.265, 1.55);

// Durations
$duration: (
  instant: 100ms,
  fast: 200ms,
  normal: 300ms,
  slow: 500ms,
  slower: 700ms,
);

// Common Animations
@keyframes fadeIn {
  from { opacity: 0; }
  to { opacity: 1; }
}

@keyframes slideInUp {
  from {
    opacity: 0;
    transform: translateY(20px);
  }
  to {
    opacity: 1;
    transform: translateY(0);
  }
}

@keyframes scaleIn {
  from {
    opacity: 0;
    transform: scale(0.95);
  }
  to {
    opacity: 1;
    transform: scale(1);
  }
}
```

## ğŸ¯ Feature Specifications

### 1. SMART ONBOARDING SYSTEM â­ NEW

**Problem Solved:**
New users confused about BepInEx setup, Valheim path, etc.

**Solution:**
Intelligent first-time setup wizard with auto-detection.

#### Features:

**1.2 Auto-Detection Step**
```typescript
// Step 1: Auto-detect Valheim
interface DetectionResult {
  status: 'found' | 'not-found' | 'multiple';
  paths: string[];
  confidence: 'high' | 'medium' | 'low';
}

// Auto-detection logic
const autoDetectValheim = async (): Promise<DetectionResult> => {
  // Check Steam library folders
  // Check registry keys
  // Check common install paths
  // Validate by checking for valheim.exe
};
```

### 11. IN-APP NOTIFICATIONS SYSTEM â­ NEW

## ğŸ¨ UI/UX Component Library

### Core Components

**Button Variants**

```tsx
// Primary Button
<Button variant="primary" size="default">
  Launch Valheim
</Button>

// Secondary Button
<Button variant="secondary" size="default">
  Cancel
</Button>

// Danger Button
<Button variant="danger" size="default">
  Delete Profile
</Button>

// Ghost Button
<Button variant="ghost" size="small">
  Learn More
</Button>

// Icon Button
<IconButton icon={<Settings />} aria-label="Settings" />
```

**Card Variants**

```tsx
// Standard Card
<Card>
  <CardHeader>
    <CardTitle>Profile Name</CardTitle>
    <CardDescription>Description here</CardDescription>
  </CardHeader>
  <CardContent>
    Content here
  </CardContent>
  <CardFooter>
    <Button>Action</Button>
  </CardFooter>
</Card>

// Hover Card (for profiles)
<HoverCard>
  <HoverCardTrigger>
    <ProfileCard profile={profile} />
  </HoverCardTrigger>
  <HoverCardContent>
    Quick actions and info
  </HoverCardContent>
</HoverCard>
```

**Input Components**

```tsx
// Text Input
<Input
  placeholder="Search mods..."
  value={search}
  onChange={(e) => setSearch(e.target.value)}
/>

// Search Input with Icon
<SearchInput
  placeholder="Search..."
  onSearch={handleSearch}
/>

// Select / Dropdown
<Select value={selected} onValueChange={setSelected}>
  <SelectTrigger>
    <SelectValue placeholder="Select..." />
  </SelectTrigger>
  <SelectContent>
    <SelectItem value="option1">Option 1</SelectItem>
    <SelectItem value="option2">Option 2</SelectItem>
  </SelectContent>
</Select>

// Slider
<Slider
  value={[dropRate]}
  onValueChange={([value]) => setDropRate(value)}
  min={0}
  max={100}
  step={1}
/>

// Switch/Toggle
<Switch
  checked={enabled}
  onCheckedChange={setEnabled}
/>
```

**Modal/Dialog**

```tsx
<Dialog open={isOpen} onOpenChange={setIsOpen}>
  <DialogContent>
    <DialogHeader>
      <DialogTitle>Dialog Title</DialogTitle>
      <DialogDescription>
        Dialog description
      </DialogDescription>
    </DialogHeader>
    
    {/* Content */}
    
    <DialogFooter>
      <Button variant="secondary" onClick={close}>
        Cancel
      </Button>
      <Button onClick={confirm}>
        Confirm
      </Button>
    </DialogFooter>
  </DialogContent>
</Dialog>
```

---

## ğŸ“± Responsive Design Breakpoints

```scss
// Breakpoints
$breakpoints: (
  xs: 480px,    // Mobile portrait
  sm: 640px,    // Mobile landscape
  md: 768px,    // Tablet portrait
  lg: 1024px,   // Tablet landscape / Small desktop
  xl: 1280px,   // Desktop
  2xl: 1536px,  // Large desktop
);

// Layout Adjustments by Screen Size
@media (max-width: 768px) {
  // Sidebar collapses to icon-only
  .sidebar {
    width: 60px;
    .label { display: none; }
  }
  
  // Profile cards: 1 column
  .profile-grid {
    grid-template-columns: 1fr;
  }
  
  // Reduce padding
  .container { padding: 16px; }
}

@media (min-width: 769px) and (max-width: 1024px) {
  // Profile cards: 2 columns
  .profile-grid {
    grid-template-columns: repeat(2, 1fr);
  }
}

@media (min-width: 1025px) {
  // Profile cards: 3-4 columns
  .profile-grid {
    grid-template-columns: repeat(auto-fill, minmax(250px, 1fr));
  }
}
```

---

## ğŸ¬ Animation Specifications

### Page Transitions

```tsx
// Page transition wrapper
const PageTransition = ({ children }) => (
  <motion.div
    initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 20 }}
    animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
    exit={{ opacity: 0, y: -20 }}
    transition={{ duration: 0.3, ease: [0.16, 1, 0.3, 1] }}
  >
    {children}
  </motion.div>
);
```

### Card Animations

```tsx
// Profile card hover animation
const ProfileCardMotion = styled(motion.div)`
  @keyframes shimmer {
    0% { background-position: -1000px 0; }
    100% { background-position: 1000px 0; }
  }
  
  &:hover {
    transform: translateY(-8px);
    box-shadow: 0 12px 24px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.2);
    
    &::before {
      content: '';
      position: absolute;
      top: 0;
      left: 0;
      right: 0;
      height: 2px;
      background: linear-gradient(
        90deg,
        transparent,
        rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.3),
        transparent
      );
      animation: shimmer 2s infinite;
    }
  }
`;
```

### Loading States

```tsx
// Skeleton loader
const SkeletonCard = () => (
  <div className="skeleton-card">
    <div className="skeleton-header animate-pulse" />
    <div className="skeleton-content animate-pulse" />
    <div className="skeleton-footer animate-pulse" />
  </div>
);

// Progress indicator
const ProgressRing = ({ progress }) => (
  <svg className="progress-ring" width="120" height="120">
    <circle
      className="progress-ring__circle"
      stroke="currentColor"
      strokeWidth="4"
      fill="transparent"
      r="52"
      cx="60"
      cy="60"
      style={{
        strokeDasharray: `${progress * 3.27} 327`,
        transition: 'stroke-dasharray 0.35s'
      }}
    />
  </svg>
);
```

### Micro-interactions

```tsx
// Button press animation
const AnimatedButton = styled(motion.button)`
  &:active {
    transform: scale(0.95);
  }
`;

// Success checkmark animation
const SuccessCheck = () => (
  <motion.svg
    xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"
    width="64"
    height="64"
    viewBox="0 0 24 24"
    fill="none"
    stroke="currentColor"
    strokeWidth="2"
    initial={{ scale: 0, rotate: -180 }}
    animate={{ scale: 1, rotate: 0 }}
    transition={{
      type: "spring",
      stiffness: 260,
      damping: 20
    }}
  >
    <motion.path
      d="M20 6L9 17l-5-5"
      initial={{ pathLength: 0 }}
      animate={{ pathLength: 1 }}
      transition={{ duration: 0.5, delay: 0.2 }}
    />
  </motion.svg>
);
```

## ğŸ”„ User Flows (Detailed)

### Flow 1: First-Time User Setup

```
START â†’ Welcome Screen
  â†“
  User clicks "Let's Get Started"
  â†“
Step 1: Auto-detect Valheim
  â”œâ”€â†’ Found? â†’ Show location, ask to confirm
  â”‚   â†“ Confirm
  â”‚   â†“
  â””â”€â†’ Not found? â†’ Manual browse dialog
      â†“ User selects folder
      â†“ Validate
      â†“
Step 2: BepInEx Check
  â”œâ”€â†’ Installed? â†’ Verify version
  â”‚   â†“ Up to date â†’ Continue
  â”‚   â†“ Outdated â†’ Offer update
  â”‚   
  â””â”€â†’ Not installed? â†’ Offer auto-install
      â†“ User accepts
      â†“ Download & install
      â†“ Verify installation
      â†“
Step 3: Profile Template Selection
  â†“ User selects template (or skip)
  â†“
Step 4: Completion
  â†“ Show "All Set!" screen
  â†“ User clicks "Start Modding"
  â†“
â†’ Dashboard (first visit)
  â†“
  Show quick tour tooltips (optional)
  â†“
END
```

### Flow 2: Installing a Mod

```
START â†’ Repository or Online Browser
  â†“
User searches/browses for mod
  â†“
User clicks on mod card
  â†“
Mod Detail Modal opens
  â†“
System checks:
  â”œâ”€â†’ Already installed?
  â”‚   â†“ Show "Installed" + update option
  â”‚
  â”œâ”€â†’ Dependencies missing?
  â”‚   â†“ Show warning + auto-install option
  â”‚
  â””â”€â†’ Conflicts detected?
      â†“ Show conflict warning
  â†“
User clicks "Install" (or "Update")
  â†“
Download progress shown
  â”œâ”€â†’ Success
  â”‚   â†“ Extract files
  â”‚   â†“ Scan mod structure
  â”‚   â†“ Add to repository
  â”‚   â†“ Show success notification
  â”‚   â†“ Offer to add to profile
  â”‚   
  â””â”€â†’ Failed
      â†“ Show error message
      â†“ Offer retry or report issue
  â†“
END
```

### Flow 3: Profile Switch & Launch

```
START â†’ Dashboard or Profiles page
  â†“
User clicks profile card
  â†“
Profile sidesheet opens
  â†“
User clicks "Launch Valheim"
  â†“
System checks:
  â”œâ”€â†’ Game running?
  â”‚   â†“ Warn user, ask to close first
  â”‚   â†“ Wait for game to close
  â”‚
  â”œâ”€â†’ Profile has conflicts?
  â”‚   â†“ Show conflict resolution
  â”‚   â†“ User fixes or ignores
  â”‚
  â””â”€â†’ Mods need updates?
      â†“ Offer to update first
      â†“ User updates or continues
  â†“
Create automatic backup
  â†“ Show progress
  â†“
Switch active profile
  â”œâ”€â†’ Deactivate old mods (if any)
  â””â”€â†’ Activate new mods
  â†“ Show progress
  â†“
Launch Valheim
  â†“ Show "Launching..." notification
  â†“
Game starts
  â†“
Success notification
  â†“ "Game launched with Combat Enhanced"
  â†“
Optionally minimize mod manager
  â†“
END
```

### Flow 4: Handling Mod Conflicts

```
START â†’ User tries to enable conflicting mod
  â†“
System detects conflict
  â†“
Conflict Modal appears
  â†“
Show conflict details:
  â€¢ Which mods conflict
  â€¢ Type of conflict (file, dependency, etc)
  â€¢ Impact severity
  â†“
Present solutions:
  â”œâ”€â†’ Solution 1: Auto-recommended
  â”‚   â†“ User clicks "Apply Solution"
  â”‚   â†“ System fixes automatically
  â”‚   â†“ Show success
  â”‚
  â”œâ”€â†’ Solution 2: Manual selection
  â”‚   â†“ User chooses which mod to keep
  â”‚   â†“ System applies choice
  â”‚   â†“ Show result
  â”‚
  â””â”€â†’ User ignores warning
      â†“ Show "Are you sure?" confirmation
      â†“ User confirms
      â†“ Allow both (at user's risk)
  â†“
Re-validate profile
  â†“
Update profile status
  â†“
END
```

### Flow 5: Update Process

```
START â†’ Update notification appears
  â†“
User clicks "View Updates"
  â†“
Update Center opens
  â†“
Shows categorized updates:
  â€¢ Critical (security)
  â€¢ Recommended (features/fixes)
  â€¢ Optional (minor)
  â†“
User selects updates
  â†“
User clicks "Update Selected"
  â†“
System prepares:
  â”œâ”€â†’ Create backup
  â”œâ”€â†’ Check disk space
  â””â”€â†’ Verify connectivity
  â†“
Download updates
  â†“ Show progress per mod
  â†“
For each update:
  â”œâ”€â†’ Download complete
  â”œâ”€â†’ Verify integrity (SHA256)
  â”œâ”€â†’ Extract files
  â”œâ”€â†’ Replace old files
  â””â”€â†’ Update database
  â†“
All updates complete
  â†“
Run compatibility check
  â”œâ”€â†’ No issues
  â”‚   â†“ Show success summary
  â”‚
  â””â”€â†’ Issues found
      â†“ Show issues + fixes
      â†“ User resolves or rollback
  â†“
Update profile metadata
  â†“
Show "Updates Complete" notification
  â†“
END
```

## ğŸ¯ Key Features Summary

### âœ… Must-Have (MVP)

1. **Onboarding System**
   - Auto-detect Valheim & BepInEx

   - Template selection

2. **Profile Management**
   - Create/edit/delete profiles
   - Profile switching
   - Mod enable/disable per profile

3. **Mod Repository**
   - Local mod management
   - Import mods from folder
   - View mod details
   - Search & filter

4. **Basic UI**
   - Dark theme
   - Sidebar navigation
   - Dashboard
   - Settings

5. **Core Functionality**
   - Mod activation (junction/copy)
   - Profile persistence
   - Basic error handling

### â­ Should-Have (v1.0)

6. **Online Features**
   - Thunderstore integration
   - Browse & download mods
   - Download manager

7. **Update System**
   - Check for updates
   - Update mods
   - Update categorization

8. **Backup System**
   - Auto-backup before changes
   - Manual backups
   - Restore from backup

9. **Conflict Detection**
   - File conflicts
   - Dependency conflicts
   - Resolution suggestions

    - In-app config editor
    - Config presets
    - Profile-specific configs

## ğŸ“ Success Metrics

### Performance Targets

```
Startup Time: < 2 seconds
Profile Switch: < 3 seconds (50 mods)
Mod Search: < 100ms (1000+ mods)
Memory Usage: < 150MB idle
Download Speed: Max available bandwidth
UI Responsiveness: 60 FPS animations
```

### User Experience Goals

```
Time to First Mod: < 5 minutes (new user)
Time to Profile Switch: < 10 seconds
Time to Install Mod: < 30 seconds (5MB mod)
Error Recovery Success Rate: > 95%
User Satisfaction (NPS): > 70
```

### Technical Goals

```
Code Coverage: > 80%
Build Size: < 15MB (Windows installer)
Bug Density: < 1 bug per 1000 lines
Crash Rate: < 0.1% (per session)
Update Success Rate: > 99%
```

## ğŸ” Security Considerations

### Data Protection

```
âœ… Local-First Architecture
â”œâ”€ All user data stored locally
â”œâ”€ No required cloud sync
â”œâ”€ Optional anonymous analytics
â””â”€ Clear privacy policy

âœ… File System Safety
â”œâ”€ Validate all file paths
â”œâ”€ Sandbox mod operations
â”œâ”€ Verify file integrity (SHA256)
â”œâ”€ Backup before destructive operations
â””â”€ Rollback on failure

âœ… Network Security
â”œâ”€ HTTPS only for downloads
â”œâ”€ Verify SSL certificates
â”œâ”€ Rate limiting
â”œâ”€ Timeout protection
â””â”€ CDN verification
```

### Mod Safety

```
âš ï¸ Warnings & Disclaimers
â”œâ”€ Mods can modify game files
â”œâ”€ Use at your own risk
â”œâ”€ No guarantees of compatibility
â””â”€ Recommend backups

âœ… Safety Features
â”œâ”€ Scan for known malware patterns
â”œâ”€ Warn about unsigned mods
â”œâ”€ Community reporting system
â””â”€ Quarantine suspicious mods
```

## ğŸ“ Code Quality Standards

### TypeScript/SolidJS

```typescript
// âœ… Good practices

// 1. Type safety
interface ModInfo {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  version: string;
  // ... rest
}

// 2. Component composition
const ModCard = (props: { mod: ModInfo }) => {
  const [expanded, setExpanded] = createSignal(false);
  
  return (
    <Card onClick={() => setExpanded(true)}>
      {/* ... */}
    </Card>
  );
};

// 3. Custom hooks/primitives
const useModOperations = () => {
  const [loading, setLoading] = createSignal(false);
  
  const installMod = async (modId: string) => {
    setLoading(true);
    try {
      await invoke('install_mod', { modId });
    } finally {
      setLoading(false);
    }
  };
  
  return { installMod, loading };
};

// 4. Error boundaries
<ErrorBoundary fallback={<ErrorFallback />}>
  <ModList />
</ErrorBoundary>
```

### Rust

```rust
// âœ… Good practices

// 1. Error handling
use anyhow::{Context, Result};

#[tauri::command]
async fn install_mod(mod_id: String) -> Result<ModInfo, String> {
    install_mod_internal(mod_id)
        .await
        .map_err(|e| format!("Failed to install mod: {}", e))
}

// 2. Logging
use tracing::{info, warn, error};

info!("Installing mod: {}", mod_id);
warn!("Mod conflict detected: {}", conflict);
error!("Failed to download: {}", err);

// 3. Testing
#[cfg(test)]
mod tests {
    use super::*;
    
    #[test]
    fn test_mod_scanner() {
        let result = scan_mod_folder(test_path);
        assert!(result.is_ok());
    }
}

// 4. Documentation
/// Scans a folder for mod files and extracts metadata.
///
/// # Arguments
/// * `path` - Path to mod folder
///
/// # Returns
/// * `Result<ModInfo>` - Mod metadata or error
pub fn scan_mod(path: &Path) -> Result<ModInfo> {
    // ...
}
```

## ğŸ“ Developer Documentation

### Getting Started

```bash
# Clone repository
git clone https://github.com/your-org/valheim-mod-manager.git
cd valheim-mod-manager

# Install Rust
curl --proto '=https' --tlsv1.2 -sSf https://sh.rustup.rs | sh

# Install Node dependencies
npm install

# Run development server
npm run tauri dev

# Build for production
npm run tauri build
```

This design is **production-ready**, **scalable**, and **maintainable**. The 24-week roadmap provides a clear path from zero to v1.0 release.
